# Text Elements
        consider an executive jet transport pattern after the Cessna 560 Citation V  show in Fig
the airplane is cruising at the speed of 492mph at an attitude of 33000ft . the ambient air density 
is                      and the weight and the wing platform areas of the plane are 15000lb and 
        . The Drag coefficients at cruise is 0.015, then calculate the lift-to-drag ratio of the plane ^NVcFdoaZ

solution:  ^FdunyM8b

For a conventional airplane almost all the lift at cruising conditions is produced by the wing. and the lift of the fuselage can be neglected. ^dfhTQkRI

Then the same plane above has a stalling speed at sea level of        at the maximum
take-off weight of 15900lb The ambient air density at standard sea level is 0.002377 
      . Then calculate the maximum lift coefficient for the airplane ^fvQywIeu

Example 1.8 ^R3Z55qFJ

Solution: ^BqCObRqI
